<span data-ttu-id="2b988-1635">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2008 R2 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2b988-1635">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
